The transit is permanently shut by default and you open to sip by pressing a spring-loaded button, which is convenient to use and definitely one-handed. I reach for my mug often when I am working on the laptop/external keyboard so the watertightness aspect is important for me. On that note, I've not noticed any leaking that reviewers are complaining about.That all said, this is still a great mug if you are happy to use two hands to close it after each sip or don't mind leaving it open, just 12 quid too. Only 4 stars from me though.My recommendation, if you are in two minds, is to go for one of their autoseal mugs - absolute peace of mind and convenience that way.\n")
